Kubernetes API server authentication chain is constructed in `pkg/kubeapiserver/authenticator/config.go` (sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0). The main entry point is `Config.New()`, which builds a slice of `authenticator.Request` objects and combines them using `union.New()` from `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/union/union.go`.\\n\\n**Authenticator Chain Construction** (`pkg/kubeapiserver/authenticator/config.go`):\\n- `Config.New()` orchestrates the chain: it creates individual authenticators and appends them to a list, then combines with `union.New()`, and wraps the result with `group.NewAuthenticatedGroupAdder()`.\\n\\n**Bearer Token Authenticator** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/bearertoken/bearertoken.go`):\\n- `Authenticator` struct wraps an `authenticator.Token` and extracts the Bearer token from the `Authorization` HTTP header. `New()` constructs it.\\n\\n**Client Certificate Authenticator** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/x509/x509.go`):\\n- `Authenticator` validates TLS client certificates and extracts user info. `NewDynamic()` is used in the chain with `CommonNameUserConversion` to map certificate common names to user identities.\\n\\n**Service Account Token Authenticator** (`pkg/serviceaccount/jwt.go`):\\n- `JWTTokenAuthenticator()` constructs a `jwtTokenAuthenticator` that validates JWT-signed service account tokens. The chain builder calls `newServiceAccountAuthenticator()` and `newLegacyServiceAccountAuthenticator()` in `pkg/kubeapiserver/authenticator/config.go`.\\n\\n**Anonymous Authenticator**
